                <ul class="top-menu"><li><a href="https://www.psx.com.pk/psx/careers">Careers</a></li><li><a href="https://dps.psx.com.pk/dataportal/daily-downloads" target="_blank">Daily Downloads</a></li></ul>
<script>
     $(document).on('change', '#month_select_futures_2', function(e) {

let month = $('#month_select_futures_2 :selected').val();

console.log(month);

let url = $(location).attr('href').split("/").splice(0, 5).join("/");
var segments = url.split( '/' );
var segment_2 = segments[4];

let limit = 0; 

if(segment_2 == 'future-contracts'){
    limit = 0; 
}else{
    limit = 1; 
}


$.ajax({
    type: "POST",
    url: 'https://www.psx.com.pk/psx/market-summary/future-contract-ajax',
    data: {
        month: month,
        limit: limit,
    },
    success: function(data) {
        if(segment_2 == 'future-contracts'){
            if (data == 'No Data found.') {
                $('#futures_table tbody').html('<h3 class="no-data-future">No Data found!</h3>');
            } else {
                data = `<tr>
                    <th>SYMBOL</th>
                    <th>OPEN</th>
                    <th>HIGH</th>
                    <th>LOW</th>
                    <th>CURRENT</th>
                    <th>CHANGE</th>
                    <th>VOLUME</th>
                </tr>` + data;
                $('#futures_table tbody').html(data);
            }
        }else{
            if (data == 'No Data found.') {$('.mkt-sum-view-all').hide();} else {
                $('.mkt-sum-view-all').show();
                $('#mkt-sum-view-btn').attr("href", "market-summary/future-contracts?type=" + month);
            }
            $('#menu1 .tbl tbody').html(data);
        }

        console.log(data);
        return false;
        // $('#activity').html(data);
    }
});

});
</script>

            </div>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('#submit_feedback_footer2').attr('id', 'submit_feedback_footer233');

    })

    $(document).on("click", "#submit_feedback_footer233", function() {
        console.log('dasdasdas');
        let name_footer = $('#name_footer').val();
        let email_footer = $('#email_footer').val();
        let query_t_footer = $('#query_t_footer').val();
        let contact_footer = $('#contact_footer').val();
        let comment_footer = $('#comment_footer').val();
        let captcha_footer = $("#ct_hiddenRecaptcha").val();
        let html = '';
        var regex = /^[0-9\s]*$/;


        if (name_footer == '' || contact_footer == '' || email_footer == '' || query_t_footer == '' || captcha_footer == '') {
            $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
            $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
            $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Fill Incomplete Fields.</h4>');
            return false;
        } else if (!regex.test(contact_footer)) {
            $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
            $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
            $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Invalid Contact.</h4>');
            return false;
        } else if (query_t_footer == '0') {
            $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
            $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
            $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Fill Incomplete Fields.</h4>');
            return false;
        } else {


            if (!isEmail(email_footer)) {
                $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Enter Valid Email Address.</h4>');
                return false;
            }
            ///alert(captcha_footer);


            $.ajax({
                type: "post",
                url: "https://www.psx.com.pk/footer_form_submit/index.php",
                dataType: 'json',
                captcha: grecaptcha.getResponse(),
                data: {
                    name: name_footer,
                    contact: contact_footer,
                    email: email_footer,
                    query_t: query_t_footer,
                    comment: comment_footer,
                    captcha: captcha_footer
                },
                success: function(data) {

                    if (data.response == "Success") {
                        $('.feed_form').load(' .feed_form');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'none');

                        //   $('#feed_form').hide(); 
                        $('.feed_form').load(" .feed_form");
                        $('.footerSuccess').html('<h4><strong> success! </strong>Thank you for feedback.</h4>');


                    } else if (data == "C") {

                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                        $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Invalid Captcha.</h4>');
                        return false;

                    } else if (data == "E") {

                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                        $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Invalid Post.</h4>');
                        return false;

                    } else if (data == "D") {

                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                        $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Fill Incomplete Fields.</h4>');
                        return false;

                    }



                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>

            margin: 0,

                    items: 1

                },

                }
            }

    $("#submit_feedback_footer2").click(function() {

        let name_footer = $('#name_footer').val();
        let email_footer = $('#email_footer').val();
        let query_t_footer = $('#query_t_footer').val();
        let contact_footer = $('#contact_footer').val();
        let comment_footer = $('#comment_footer').val();
        let captcha_footer = $("#ct_hiddenRecaptcha").val();
        let html = '';
        var regex = /^[0-9\s]*$/;


        if (name_footer == '' || contact_footer == '' || email_footer == '' || query_t_footer == '' || captcha_footer == '') {
            $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
            $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
            $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Fill Incomplete Fields.</h4>');
            return false;
        } else if (!regex.test(contact_footer)) {
            $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
            $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
            $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Invalid Contact.</h4>');
            return false;
        } else if (query_t_footer == '0') {
            $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
            $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
            $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Fill Incomplete Fields.</h4>');
            return false;
        } else {


            if (!isEmail(email_footer)) {
                $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Enter Valid Email Address.</h4>');
                return false;
            }
            ///alert(captcha_footer);


            $.ajax({
                type: "post",
                url: "footer_form_submit/index.php",
                dataType: 'json',
                captcha: grecaptcha.getResponse(),
                data: {
                    name: name_footer,
                    contact: contact_footer,
                    email: email_footer,
                    query_t: query_t_footer,
                    comment: comment_footer,
                    captcha: captcha_footer
                },
                success: function(data) {

                    if (data.response == "Success") {
                        $('.feed_form').load(' .feed_form');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'none');

                        //   $('#feed_form').hide(); 
                        $('.feed_form').load(" .feed_form");
                        $('.footerSuccess').html('<h4><strong> success! </strong>Thank you for feedback.</h4>');


                    } else if (data == "C") {

                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                        $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Invalid Captcha.</h4>');
                        return false;

                    } else if (data == "E") {

                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                        $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Invalid Post.</h4>');
                        return false;

                    } else if (data == "D") {

                        $('.footerDanger').css('display', 'block');
                        $('.footerSuccess').css('display', 'none');
                        $('.footerDanger').html('<h4><strong> Error! </strong> Please Fill Incomplete Fields.</h4>');
                        return false;

                    }



                }
            });
        }
    });
</script>
